40  
41  public class IBM970_OLD
42      extends Charset
43      implements HistoricallyNamedCharset
44  {
45  
46      private final static IBM970 nioCoder = new IBM970();
47  
48      public IBM970_OLD() {
49          super("x-IBM970-Old", null);
50      }
51  
52      public String historicalName() {
53          return "Cp970";
54      }
55  
56      public boolean contains(Charset cs) {
57          return (cs instanceof IBM970);
58      }
59  
60      public CharsetDecoder newDecoder() {
61          return new Decoder(this);
62      }
63  
64      public CharsetEncoder newEncoder() {
65          return new Encoder(this);
66      }
67  
68      public String getDecoderSingleByteMappings() {
69          return Decoder.byteToCharTable;
70      }
71  
72      public String getDecoderMappingTableG1() {
73          return Decoder.mappingTableG1;
74      }
75  
76      public short[] getEncoderIndex1() {
77          return Encoder.index1;
78  
79      }
80      public String getEncoderIndex2() {
81          return Encoder.index2;
82  
83      }
84      public String getEncoderIndex2a() {
85          return Encoder.index2a;
86      }

1212                 "\u8208\u50D6\u51DE\u559C\u566B\u56CD\u59EC\u5B09" +
1213                 "\u5E0C\u6199\u6198\u6231\u665E\u66E6\u7199\u71B9" +
1214                 "\u71BA\u72A7\u79A7\u7A00\u7FB2\u8A70\uE05E\uE05F" +
1215                 "\uE060\uE061\uE062\uE063\uE064\uE065\uE066\uE067" +
1216                 "\uE068\uE069\uE06A\uE06B\uE06C\uE06D\uE06E\uE06F" +
1217                 "\uE070\uE071\uE072\uE073\uE074\uE075\uE076\uE077" +
1218                 "\uE078\uE079\uE07A\uE07B\uE07C\uE07D\uE07E\uE07F" +
1219                 "\uE080\uE081\uE082\uE083\uE084\uE085\uE086\uE087" +
1220                 "\uE088\uE089\uE08A\uE08B\uE08C\uE08D\uE08E\uE08F" +
1221                 "\uE090\uE091\uE092\uE093\uE094\uE095\uE096\uE097" +
1222                 "\uE098\uE099\uE09A\uE09B\uE09C\uE09D\uE09E\uE09F" +
1223                 "\uE0A0\uE0A1\uE0A2\uE0A3\uE0A4\uE0A5\uE0A6\uE0A7" +
1224                 "\uE0A8\uE0A9\uE0AA\uE0AB\uE0AC\uE0AD\uE0AE\uE0AF" +
1225                 "\uE0B0\uE0B1\uE0B2\uE0B3\uE0B4\uE0B5\uE0B6\uE0B7" +
1226                 "\uE0B8\uE0B9\uE0BA\uE0BB"
1227                 ;
1228         }
1229     }
1230 
1231     protected static class Encoder extends CharsetEncoder {
1232 
1233         private static final char SBase = '\uAC00';
1234         private static final char LBase = '\u1100';
1235         private static final char VBase = '\u1161';
1236         private static final char TBase = '\u11A7';
1237         private static final int  VCount = 21;
1238         private static final int  TCount = 28;
1239         private static final byte G0 = 0;
1240         private static final byte G1 = 1;
1241         private static final byte G2 = 2;
1242         private static final byte G3 = 3;
1243         private byte   charState = G0;
1244         private char   l, v, t;
1245         private int mask1 , mask2, shift;
1246 
1247         private final Surrogate.Parser sgp = new Surrogate.Parser();
1248 
1249         public Encoder(Charset cs) {
1250             super(cs, 2.0f, 2.0f);
1251             mask1 = 0xFFF8;
1252             mask2 = 0x0007;
1253             shift = 3;
1254         }
1255 
1256         /**
1257          * Returns true if the given character can be converted to the
1258          * target character encoding.
1259          */
1260         public boolean canEncode(char ch) {
1261            int  index;
1262            int  theBytes;
1263 
1264            //The underneath data table returns a non-zero value for
1265            //some surrogates, here is the workaround.
1266            if (Surrogate.is(ch))
1267                return false;
1268 
1269            index = index1[((ch & mask1) >> shift)] + (ch & mask2);
1270            if (index < 15000)
1271              theBytes = (int)(index2.charAt(index));
1272            else
1273              theBytes = (int)(index2a.charAt(index-15000));
1274 
1275            if (theBytes != 0)
1276               return (true);
1277 
1278            // only return true if input char was unicode null - all others are
1279            //    undefined
1280            return( ch == '\u0000');
1281         }
1282 
1283         private CoderResult encodeArrayLoop(CharBuffer src, ByteBuffer dst) {
1284             char[] sa = src.array();
1285             int sp = src.arrayOffset() + src.position();
1286             int sl = src.arrayOffset() + src.limit();
1287             byte[] da = dst.array();
1288             int dp = dst.arrayOffset() + dst.position();
1289             int dl = dst.arrayOffset() + dst.limit();
1290             int outputSize = 0;         // size of output
1291             byte[] outputBytes = new byte[2];
1292 
1293             boolean needsFlushing = false;
1294 
1295             try {
1296                 while (sp < sl) {
1297                 char inputChar = sa[sp];
1298 
1299                 // Reject surrogates
1300                 if (sgp.parse(inputChar, sa, sp, sl) < 0)
1301                     return sgp.error();
1302                 if (Surrogate.is(inputChar))
1303                         return sgp.unmappableResult();
1304 
1305                 switch (charState) {
1306                 case G0:
1307                     l = LBase;
1308                     v = VBase;
1309                     t = TBase;
1310 
1311                     if ( isLeadingC(inputChar) ) {     // Leading Consonant
1312                         l = inputChar;
1313                         charState = G1;
1314                         break;
1315                     }
1316 
1317                     if ( isVowel(inputChar) ) {        // Vowel
1318                         v = inputChar;
1319                         charState = G2;
1320                         break;
1321                     }
1322 
1323                     if ( isTrailingC(inputChar) ) {    // Trailing Consonant
1324                         t = inputChar;
1325                         charState = G3;
1326                         break;
1327                     }
1328 
1329                     break;
1330 
1331                     case G1:
1332                         if ( isLeadingC(inputChar) ) {     // Leading Consonant
1333                             l = composeLL(l, inputChar);
1334                             needsFlushing = true;
1335                         break;
1336                         }
1337 
1338                         if ( isVowel(inputChar) ) {        // Vowel
1339                             v = inputChar;
1340                             charState = G2;
1341                             needsFlushing = true;
1342                             break;
1343                         }
1344 
1345                         if ( isTrailingC(inputChar) ) {    // Trailing Consonant
1346                             t = inputChar;
1347                             charState = G3;
1348                             needsFlushing = true;
1349                             break;
1350                         }
1351 
1352                         charState = G0;
1353                         break;
1354 
1355                     case G2:
1356                         if ( isLeadingC(inputChar) ) {     // Leading Consonant
1357                             needsFlushing = true;
1358 
1359                             l = inputChar;
1360                             v = VBase;
1361                             t = TBase;
1362                             charState = G1;
1363                             break;
1364                         }
1365 
1366                         if ( isVowel(inputChar) ) {        // Vowel
1367                             needsFlushing = true;
1368                             v = composeVV(l, inputChar);
1369                             charState = G2;
1370                             break;
1371                         }
1372 
1373                         if ( isTrailingC(inputChar) ) {    // Trailing Consonant
1374                             needsFlushing = true;
1375                             t = inputChar;
1376                             charState = G3;
1377                             break;
1378                         }
1379 
1380                         charState = G0;
1381                         break;
1382 
1383                     case G3:
1384                         if ( isTrailingC(inputChar) ) {    // Trailing Consonant
1385                             needsFlushing = true;
1386                             t = composeTT(t, inputChar);
1387                             charState = G3;
1388                             break;
1389                         }
1390 
1391                         charState = G0;
1392                         break;
1393                   }
1394 
1395                   if (charState == G0 || (sl - sp < 2)) {
1396                       int spaceNeeded;
1397 
1398                         if (needsFlushing) {
1399                             needsFlushing = false;
1400                             outputBytes = encodeHangul(composeHangul());
1401 
1402                             if (outputBytes[0] == 0x00 && outputBytes[1] == 0x00
1403                                 && inputChar != '\u0000') {
1404                                   return CoderResult.unmappableForLength(1);
1405                             }
1406 
1407                             if (outputBytes[0] == 0x00)
1408                                 spaceNeeded = 1;
1409                             else
1410                                 spaceNeeded = 2;
1411 
1412                             if (dl - dp < spaceNeeded)
1413                                  return CoderResult.OVERFLOW;
1414                               if (spaceNeeded == 1)
1415                                     da[dp++] = outputBytes[1];
1416                               else {
1417                                     da[dp++] = outputBytes[0];
1418                                     da[dp++] = outputBytes[1];
1419                               }
1420                            }
1421                         outputBytes = encodeHangul(inputChar);
1422                         if (outputBytes[0] == 0x00 && outputBytes[1] == 0x00
1423                             && inputChar != '\u0000') {
1424                               return CoderResult.unmappableForLength(1);
1425                         }
1426 
1427                         if (outputBytes[0] == 0x00)
1428                             spaceNeeded = 1;
1429                         else
1430                             spaceNeeded = 2;
1431 
1432                         if (dl - dp < spaceNeeded) {
1433                              return CoderResult.OVERFLOW;
1434                         }
1435                           if (spaceNeeded == 1)
1436                                 da[dp++] = outputBytes[1];
1437                           else {
1438                                 da[dp++] = outputBytes[0];
1439                                     da[dp++] = outputBytes[1];
1440                               }
1441                         }
1442                   sp++;
1443                 }
1444                 return CoderResult.UNDERFLOW;
1445             } finally {
1446                 src.position(sp - src.arrayOffset());
1447                 dst.position(dp - dst.arrayOffset());
1448             }
1449         }
1450 
1451         private CoderResult encodeBufferLoop(CharBuffer src, ByteBuffer dst) {
1452             int mark = src.position();
1453             int outputSize = 0;
1454             byte[] outputBytes = new byte[2];
1455             boolean needsFlushing = false;
1456 
1457             try {
1458                 while (src.hasRemaining()) {
1459                     char inputChar = src.get();
1460                     if (Surrogate.is(inputChar)) {
1461                         if (sgp.parse(inputChar, src) < 0)
1462                             return sgp.error();
1463                     return sgp.unmappableResult();
1464                     }
1465 
1466                     if (inputChar >= '\uFFFE')
1467                         return CoderResult.unmappableForLength(1);
1468 
1469                     switch (charState) {
1470                     case G0:
1471                         l = LBase;
1472                         v = VBase;
1473                         t = TBase;
1474 
1475                         if ( isLeadingC(inputChar) ) {     // Leading Consonant
1476                             l = inputChar;
1477                             charState = G1;
1478                             break;
1479                         }
1480 
1481                         if ( isVowel(inputChar) ) {        // Vowel
1482                             v = inputChar;
1483                             charState = G2;
1484                             break;
1485                         }
1486 
1487                         if ( isTrailingC(inputChar) ) {    // Trailing Consonant
1488                             t = inputChar;
1489                             charState = G3;
1490                             break;
1491                         }
1492 
1493                         break;
1494 
1495                         case G1:
1496                             if ( isLeadingC(inputChar) ) {     // Leading Consonant
1497                                 l = composeLL(l, inputChar);
1498                                 needsFlushing = true;
1499                             break;
1500                             }
1501 
1502                             if ( isVowel(inputChar) ) {        // Vowel
1503                                 v = inputChar;
1504                                 charState = G2;
1505                                 needsFlushing = true;
1506                                 break;
1507                             }
1508 
1509                             if ( isTrailingC(inputChar) ) {    // Trailing Consonant
1510                                 t = inputChar;
1511                                 charState = G3;
1512                                 needsFlushing = true;
1513                                 break;
1514                             }
1515 
1516                             charState = G0;
1517                             break;
1518 
1519                         case G2:
1520                             if ( isLeadingC(inputChar) ) {     // Leading Consonant
1521                                 needsFlushing = true;
1522 
1523                                 l = inputChar;
1524                                 v = VBase;
1525                                 t = TBase;
1526                                 charState = G1;
1527                                 break;
1528                             }
1529 
1530                             if ( isVowel(inputChar) ) {        // Vowel
1531                                 needsFlushing = true;
1532                                 v = composeVV(l, inputChar);
1533                                 charState = G2;
1534                                 break;
1535                             }
1536 
1537                             if ( isTrailingC(inputChar) ) {    // Trailing Consonant
1538                                 needsFlushing = true;
1539                                 t = inputChar;
1540                                 charState = G3;
1541                                 break;
1542                             }
1543 
1544                             charState = G0;
1545                             break;
1546 
1547                         case G3:
1548                             if ( isTrailingC(inputChar) ) {    // Trailing Consonant
1549                                 needsFlushing = true;
1550                                 t = composeTT(t, inputChar);
1551                                 charState = G3;
1552                                 break;
1553                             }
1554 
1555                             charState = G0;
1556                             break;
1557                       }
1558 
1559                       if (charState == G0 || src.remaining() <= 0) {
1560                           int spaceNeeded;
1561 
1562                           if (needsFlushing) {
1563                             needsFlushing = false;
1564 
1565                             outputBytes = encodeHangul(composeHangul());
1566                             if (outputBytes[0] == 0x00
1567                                 && outputBytes[1] == 0x00
1568                                 && inputChar != '\u0000') {
1569                                 return CoderResult.unmappableForLength(1);
1570                             }
1571 
1572                             if (outputBytes[0] == 0x00)
1573                                 spaceNeeded = 1;
1574                             else
1575                                 spaceNeeded = 2;
1576 
1577                             if (dst.remaining() < spaceNeeded)
1578                                  return CoderResult.OVERFLOW;
1579                               if (spaceNeeded == 1)
1580                                     dst.put(outputBytes[1]);
1581                               else {
1582                                     dst.put(outputBytes[0]);
1583                                     dst.put(outputBytes[1]);
1584                               }
1585                           }
1586 
1587                           outputBytes = encodeHangul(inputChar);
1588                           if (outputBytes[0] == 0x00 && outputBytes[1] == 0x00
1589                               && inputChar != '\u0000') {
1590                               return CoderResult.unmappableForLength(1);
1591                           }
1592 
1593                           if (outputBytes[0] == 0x00)
1594                               spaceNeeded = 1;
1595                           else
1596                               spaceNeeded = 2;
1597 
1598                           if (dst.remaining() < spaceNeeded)
1599                                 return CoderResult.OVERFLOW;
1600 
1601                           if (spaceNeeded == 1)
1602                                 dst.put(outputBytes[1]);
1603                           else {
1604                                 dst.put(outputBytes[0]);
1605                                 dst.put(outputBytes[1]);
1606                             }
1607                         }
1608                       mark++;
1609                 }
1610                 return CoderResult.UNDERFLOW;
1611             } finally {
1612                 src.position(mark);
1613             }
1614         }
1615 
1616         private char composeHangul() {
1617            int lIndex, vIndex, tIndex;
1618 
1619            lIndex = l - LBase;
1620            vIndex = v - VBase;
1621            tIndex = t - TBase;
1622 
1623            return (char)((lIndex * VCount + vIndex) * TCount + tIndex + SBase);
1624         }
1625 
1626         private char composeLL(char l1, char l2) {
1627            return l2;
1628         }
1629 
1630         private char composeVV(char v1, char v2) {
1631            return v2;
1632         }
1633 
1634         private char composeTT(char t1, char t2) {
1635            return t2;
1636         }
1637 
1638         private boolean isLeadingC(char c) {
1639            return (c >= LBase && c <= '\u1159');
1640         }
1641 
1642         private boolean isVowel(char c) {
1643            return (c >= VBase && c <= '\u11a2');
1644         }
1645 
1646         private boolean isTrailingC(char c) {
1647            return (c >= TBase && c <= '\u11f9');
1648         }
1649 
1650         private byte[] encodeHangul(char unicode) {
1651             int index;
1652             byte[] outputBytes = new byte[2];
1653 
1654             int theBytes;
1655 
1656             // first we convert the unicode to its byte representation
1657 
1658             index = index1[((unicode & mask1) >> shift)] + (unicode & mask2);
1659             if (index < 15000)
1660              theBytes = (int)(index2.charAt(index));
1661             else
1662              theBytes = (int)(index2a.charAt(index-15000));
1663 
1664             outputBytes[0] = (byte)((theBytes & 0x0000ff00)>>8);
1665             outputBytes[1] = (byte)(theBytes & 0x000000ff);
1666 
1667             return outputBytes;
1668         }
1669 
1670         protected CoderResult encodeLoop(CharBuffer src, ByteBuffer dst) {
1671             if (true && src.hasArray() && dst.hasArray())
1672                 return encodeArrayLoop(src, dst);
1673             else
1674                 return encodeBufferLoop(src, dst);
1675         }
1676
